    <script>
        if(!String.prototype.trim) {
            try {
                var keyword = "";
                if(decodeURI(window.location.search).indexOf("?") != -1 && decodeURI(window.location.search).substr(1).match(new RegExp("(^|&)"+ "keyword" +"=([^&]*)(&|$)")) != null && decodeURI(window.location.search).substr(1).match(new RegExp("(^|&)"+ "keyword" +"=([^&]*)(&|$)"))[2] != null) {
                    keyword = encodeURIComponent(decodeURIComponent(String(decodeURI(window.location.search).substr(1).match(new RegExp("(^|&)"+ "keyword" +"=([^&]*)(&|$)"))[2])));
                }
                window.location.href= "//www.sogou.com/sogou?query=" + keyword
            } catch (err) {
                console.error(err);
            }
        }
    </script>
